				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Himmelskönig, sei willkommen, BWV 182 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>

<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1714-28 in Weimar
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Himmelskönig, sei willkommen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">King of Heaven, be Thou welcome
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ca">Himmelskönig</span>; <span title="he">Himmelskönig, sei willkommen, רי"ב 182</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/180237500">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Himmelsk%C3%B6nig,_sei_willkommen,_BWV_182">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/180237500">180237500</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n83073633">n83073633</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300008872">300008872</a>; <span class="expandline" title="2 more..."><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13939765f">13939765f</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Library_of_Australia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:National Library of Australia">NLA</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://nla.gov.au/anbd.aut-an35672964">35672964</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 182&#160;; BC A 53, BC A 172
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 293
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major (1714); G&#160;major (other versions)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 movements:
<ol><li>Sonata
</li><li>Chorus: Himmelskönig, sei willkommen
</li><li>Recitative (bass): Siehe, ich komme, im Buch ist von mir geschrieben
</li><li>Aria (bass): Starkes Lieben
</li><li>Aria (alto): Leget euch dem Heiland unter
</li><li>Aria (tenor): Jesu, laß durch Wohl und Weh
</li><li>Chorus: Jesu, deine Passion ist mir lauter Freude
</li><li>Chorale: So lasset uns gehen in Salem der Freuden
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1714-28 in Weimar
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1714-03-25 in Weimar (1st Performance)<br />1717-23 in Weimar (2nd/3rd Performances)<br />1724-03-25 in Leipzig (4th Performance)<br />1728-03-21 in Leipzig (5th Performance)<br />1728 (after) (6th Performance)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1843 in Berlin
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>

</dd></dl>
